### 2. Api Design Consistency
**Rule:** API documentation and payloads should be semantically accurate, future-proof, and include human-readable fields. Avoid implementation-specific details in docs, ensure required fields are never silently empty, and use consistent PATCH semantics.

**Category:** api-design
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.4
**Review count:** 4
**Source PRs:** #47200, #47212, #47255
**Modules:** nucleus, apps, extensions, global
**Trigger:** When writing or modifying API schemas, documentation, PATCH endpoints, or audit event payloads
**Rationale:** Implementation-specific docs break when internals change. Silently empty required fields confuse API consumers. Missing human-readable names force users to do extra lookups. Reviewers consistently flag these across nucleus, apps, and extensions.

---

### 3. Fail Explicitly
**Rule:** When a method encounters an unsupported type, impossible state, or unresolvable required field, throw an explicit error rather than silently returning empty/no-op results or continuing execution.

**Category:** error-handling
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.3
**Review count:** 3
**Source PRs:** #47189, #47216
**Modules:** apps
**Trigger:** When handling unexpected types in match/switch expressions, resolving required fields that may be absent, or encountering states that should be impossible
**Rationale:** Silent returns mask bugs and make debugging harder. Three instances across two PRs from different reviewers show this is a strongly-held team convention. Reviewers explicitly asked for throws over silent skips.

---

### 4. Push Sorting Filtering To Db
**Rule:** Sorting, pagination, and relational lookups should be performed in database queries, not in application memory. Avoid N+1 query patterns by combining lookups into single query pipelines.

**Category:** performance
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.3
**Review count:** 3
**Source PRs:** #47189, #47212
**Modules:** apps
**Trigger:** When implementing list endpoints with sorting or pagination, joining related entities, or fetching collections that are filtered or sorted after retrieval
**Rationale:** In-memory sorting of unbounded collections causes performance degradation at scale. N+1 queries multiply latency. Reviewers explicitly asked to push sorting/paging into persister methods and combine lookups into single query pipelines.

---

### 5. Logging Level Correctness
**Rule:** Routine operational messages should use DEBUG, not INFO. Warnings should only fire on genuinely unexpected conditions, and log messages must accurately reflect the condition that triggers them.

**Category:** logging
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.3
**Review count:** 3
**Source PRs:** #47170, #47216, #47233
**Modules:** server, apps
**Trigger:** When adding or modifying log statements, especially when choosing between INFO/DEBUG/WARN levels or writing log message text
**Rationale:** Overly verbose INFO logs create noise in production. Warnings on legitimate conditions cause alert fatigue. Inaccurate log messages mislead on-call engineers. Reviewers enforce logging discipline across multiple PRs.

---

### 6. Handle Absent Entities
**Rule:** When code looks up an entity that may not exist (deleted, archived, never created), handle the absence explicitly — clean up stale references, provide fallback behavior, or defend against null returns.

**Category:** error-handling
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.3
**Review count:** 3
**Source PRs:** #47170, #47189, #47216
**Modules:** server, apps
**Trigger:** When fetching entities by ID that could be deleted, archived, or not yet created, or when processing collections that reference other entities
**Rationale:** Unhandled absent entities cause NullPointerExceptions or stale data in indexes. Reviewers flagged cases where archived apps remained in search indexes and where missing instances or commits had no fallback handling.

---

### 7. Documentation Discipline
**Rule:** TODOs must reference tracked tickets. Forward-looking assumptions must be documented inline. Interface-layer docs must not reference implementation details from other modules.

**Category:** documentation
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.3
**Review count:** 3
**Source PRs:** #47178, #47189, #47216
**Modules:** server, apps
**Trigger:** When adding TODO comments, writing docstrings on interface-layer classes, or making assumptions about current system behavior that may change
**Rationale:** Untracked TODOs are never resolved. Undocumented assumptions become invisible tech debt. Cross-module implementation details in interface docs create coupling and break when internals change.

---

### 8. Pass Function References Directly
**Rule:** Pass function references directly as callbacks instead of wrapping them in unnecessary arrow functions.

**Category:** performance
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.3
**Review count:** 3
**Source PRs:** #40893
**Modules:** frontend

---

### 9. Constructor Dependency Injection
**Rule:** Dependencies must be injected via class constructor arguments rather than instantiated inside the class, to enable unit testing.

**Category:** architecture
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.3
**Review count:** 3
**Source PRs:** #40643
**Modules:** model-serving

---

### 10. Actionable User Error Messages
**Rule:** Error messages shown to users should explain the probable cause in plain language and suggest resolution steps. Don't surface raw internal errors.

**Category:** error-handling
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.2
**Review count:** 2
**Source PRs:** #47178, #47189
**Modules:** server, apps
**Trigger:** When writing error messages that will be displayed in the UI or returned in user-facing API responses
**Rationale:** Raw internal errors confuse users and generate support tickets. Reviewers asked for messages like 'User hasn't logged in yet' instead of technical errors, so users can self-resolve.

---

### 11. Encode Required Fields Non Optional
**Rule:** Fields required for operation should be non-optional types. When fields are nullable at creation but resolved at runtime, resolve and persist them before execution to ensure reproducibility.

**Category:** architecture
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.2
**Review count:** 2
**Source PRs:** #47189
**Modules:** apps
**Trigger:** When defining case classes or data models where fields are Optional but always expected to have values at execution time
**Rationale:** Optional types for required fields push validation to every call site. Unresolved nullable fields at execution time break reproducibility. Reviewer asked to make non-optional fields actually non-optional in case classes and resolve all such fields before launching.

---

### 12. Test Edge Cases And Transitions
**Rule:** When introducing new allowed behaviors or wrapping service calls in NonFatal recovery, add explicit tests for those specific scenarios.

**Category:** testing
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.2
**Review count:** 2
**Source PRs:** #47189, #47212
**Modules:** server, apps
**Trigger:** When adding new state transitions, changing allowed behaviors between entities, or adding error recovery wrappers around service calls
**Rationale:** New behaviors without tests are invisible regressions waiting to happen. Reviewers specifically asked for tests covering new allowed version transitions and fallback behavior when taxonomy service fails.

---

### 13. Prefer Lodash Es Over Lodash

**Category:** performance
**Mode:** ambient
**Confidence:** 0.2
**Review count:** 2

### 15. Await Async Functions In Try Catch
**Rule:** Always await async function calls inside try-catch blocks; unawaited async calls will not have their errors caught by the surrounding try-catch.
